M\u1ed9t th\u1eddi gian sau, c\u00e1c th\u01b0\u01a1ng nh\u00e2n b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u \u0111\u1ec3 \u00fd v\u00e0 ph\u00e1t hi\u1ec7n ra, h\u1ecd sinh nghi ng\u1edd, th\u1ebf l\u00e0 h\u1ecd \u0111\u1ed3ng lo\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ebfn ti\u00eam g\u1eedi v\u00e0ng \u0111\u1ec3 r\u00fat v\u00e0ng. H\u01a1n n\u1eefa, Hoa K\u1ef3 \u0111\u00e3 nh\u1eafm m\u1ee5c ti\u00eau v\u00e0o to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 ng\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng nghi\u1ec7p ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed, t\u1eadp trung n\u1ed7 l\u1ef1c ch\u1ed1ng l\u1ea1i c\u00e1c m\u1ed1i li\u00ean h\u1ec7 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c d\u1ef1 \u0111o\u00e1n c\u1ee7a t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed v\u1edbi c\u00e1c ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng t\u1ed9i ph\u1ea1m.\n\n\u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y \u0111\u00e3 th\u00fac \u0111\u1ea9y nh\u1eefng n\u1ed7 l\u1ef1c hi\u1ec7n t\u1ea1i c\u1ee7a c\u01a1 quan c\u00f3 th\u1ea9m quy\u1ec1n trong vi\u1ec7c \u0111\u01b0a stablecoin v\u00e0o khung ph\u00e1p l\u00fd nh\u01b0 m\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n trong nh\u1eefng thay \u0111\u1ed5i ng\u00e0y c\u00e0ng t\u0103ng c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd. Quy \u0111\u1ecbnh v\u1ec1 ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed \u0111\u00e3 tr\u1edf th\u00e0nh ch\u1ee7 \u0111\u1ec1 k\u1ec3 t\u1eeb \u0111\u1ea7u n\u0103m, sau s\u1ef1 s\u1ee5p \u0111\u1ed5 g\u1ea7n \u0111\u00e2y c\u1ee7a c\u00f4ng ty s\u00e0n giao d\u1ecbch ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed FTX khi\u1ebfn to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 c\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed b\u1ecb t\u1ed5n th\u01b0\u01a1ng.\u00a0\n\n\u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y l\u00e0m t\u0103ng s\u1ef1 ch\u00fa \u00fd c\u1ee7a ch\u00ednh ph\u1ee7 \u0111\u1ed1i v\u1edbi t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1. M\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n c\u1ee7a qu\u00e1 tr\u00ecnh t\u1ed1 t\u1ee5ng n\u00e0y l\u00e0 vi\u1ec7c Capitol Hill ng\u00e0y c\u00e0ng ch\u00fa \u00fd h\u01a1n \u0111\u1ebfn vi\u1ec7c ho\u1ea1ch \u0111\u1ecbnh ch\u00ednh s\u00e1ch c\u1ee7a ng\u00e0nh ti\u1ec1n k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1. Xem x\u00e9t s\u1ef1 ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n ng\u00e0y c\u00e0ng t\u0103ng, c\u00e1c nh\u00e0 l\u1eadp ph\u00e1p v\u00e0 c\u00e1c c\u01a1 quan trung \u01b0\u01a1ng kh\u00e1c tr\u00ean to\u00e0n th\u1ebf gi\u1edbi \u0111ang ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn giai \u0111o\u1ea1n m\u1edbi n\u00e0y c\u1ee7a ng\u00e0nh v\u1edbi nhi\u1ec1u lo ng\u1ea1i.\n\nT\u00ecnh c\u1ea3m v\u1ec1 quy \u0111\u1ecbnh c\u1ee7a stablecoin\n\nTheo th\u00f4ng b\u00e1o h\u00f4m th\u1ee9 S\u00e1u c\u1ee7a C\u1ee5c D\u1ef1 tr\u1eef Li\u00ean bang, stablecoin c\u1ea7n ph\u1ea3i \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd nh\u01b0 m\u1ed9t ph\u1ea7n c\u1ee7a khu\u00f4n kh\u1ed5 ng\u00e0y c\u00e0ng t\u0103ng trong vi\u1ec7c \u00e1p d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c lo\u1ea1i ti\u1ec1n k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1 v\u00e0 Michael Barr t\u1eadp trung nhi\u1ec1u h\u01a1n v\u00e0o c\u00e1c lo\u1ea1i ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ch\u00ednh ph\u1ee7 b\u1ea3o \u0111\u1ea3m.\n\nTheo Barr, nh\u1eefng lo\u1ea1i ti\u1ec1n t\u1ec7 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ch\u1ed1t n\u00e0y ng\u1ee5 \u00fd r\u1eb1ng nh\u1eefng t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n n\u00e0y l\u00e0 \u201cs\u1ef1 tin t\u01b0\u1edfng vay m\u01b0\u1ee3n c\u1ee7a ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng trung \u01b0\u01a1ng\u201d, \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y t\u1ea1o ra nhu c\u1ea7u v\u1ec1 c\u00e1c lu\u1eadt v\u00e0 quy \u0111\u1ecbnh c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft. Anh \u1ea5y n\u00f3i th\u00eam:\nC\u1ee5c D\u1ef1 tr\u1eef Li\u00ean bang r\u1ea5t quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn vi\u1ec7c \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o r\u1eb1ng m\u1ecdi d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 stablecoin \u0111\u1ec1u ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng trong khu\u00f4n kh\u1ed5 gi\u00e1m s\u00e1t an to\u00e0n th\u00edch h\u1ee3p c\u1ee7a li\u00ean bang, \u0111\u1ec3 ch\u00fang kh\u00f4ng \u0111e d\u1ecda \u0111\u1ebfn s\u1ef1 \u1ed5n \u0111\u1ecbnh t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh ho\u1eb7c t\u00ednh to\u00e0n v\u1eb9n c\u1ee7a h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng thanh to\u00e1n.\n                                                                       Michael Barr\n\nNgo\u00e0i ra, Hoa K\u1ef3 \u0111\u00e3 b\u00ecnh lu\u1eadn v\u1ec1 vi\u1ec7c t\u0103ng c\u01b0\u1eddng gi\u00e1m s\u00e1t c\u00e1c ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng stablecoin. Barr b\u00e0y t\u1ecf s\u1ef1 lo l\u1eafng c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh v\u1ec1 nh\u1eefng t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c c\u01a1 quan li\u00ean bang gi\u00e1m s\u00e1t.\n\n\u00d4ng c\u0169ng tham gia b\u00ecnh lu\u1eadn v\u1ec1 Ti\u1ec1n t\u1ec7 k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1 c\u1ee7a Ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng Trung \u01b0\u01a1ng (CBDC) b\u1edfi Ng\u00e0i Jon Cunliffe, hi\u1ec7n l\u00e0 c\u1ef1u Ph\u00f3 th\u1ed1ng \u0111\u1ed1c Ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng Anh (BOE), khi \u00f4ng c\u00f3 b\u00e0i ph\u00e1t bi\u1ec3u cu\u1ed1i c\u00f9ng t\u1ea1i h\u1ed9i ngh\u1ecb. Nhi\u1ec7m k\u1ef3 10 n\u0103m c\u1ee7a Cunliffe k\u1ebft th\u00fac v\u00e0o ng\u00e0y 31 th\u00e1ng 10 v\u00e0 \u00f4ng c\u0169ng nh\u1ea5n m\u1ea1nh r\u1eb1ng ch\u01b0a c\u00f3 quy\u1ebft \u0111\u1ecbnh n\u00e0o v\u1ec1 CBDC \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u0111\u01b0a ra \u1edf Anh.\n\nTuy nhi\u00ean, trong m\u1ed9t b\u00e0i vi\u1ebft t\u01b0 v\u1ea5n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c xu\u1ea5t b\u1ea3n v\u00e0o \u0111\u1ea7u n\u0103m nay, Cunliffe \u0111\u00e3 th\u1ec3 hi\u1ec7n s\u1ef1 quan t\u00e2m c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh \u0111\u1ed1i v\u1edbi CBDC v\u00e0 k\u1ebft lu\u1eadn r\u1eb1ng \u00f4ng \u0111\u00e3 nh\u1eadn \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c h\u01a1n 50.000 ph\u1ea3n h\u1ed3i. \u00d4ng \u0111\u00e3 h\u00ecnh dung: \u201cC\u00e1c c\u00f4ng ty t\u01b0 nh\u00e2n s\u1ebd c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u00edch h\u1ee3p v\u00e0 l\u1eadp tr\u00ecnh B\u1ea3ng k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1, l\u00e0m t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n thanh to\u00e1n, v\u00e0o c\u00e1c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 m\u00e0 h\u1ecd s\u1ebd cung c\u1ea5p cho ch\u1ee7 s\u1edf h\u1eefu v\u00ed\u201d. Cunliffe c\u0169ng n\u00f3i th\u00eam:\nT\u00f4i s\u1ebd quan s\u00e1t, n\u1ebfu ch\u1ec9 n\u00f3i \u0111\u00f9a m\u1ed9t ch\u00fat, r\u1eb1ng nh\u1eefng l\u1eddi ch\u1ec9 tr\u00edch v\u1ec1 \u0110\u1ed3ng B\u1ea3ng K\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1 \u0111\u00e3 thay \u0111\u1ed5i t\u1eeb lo ng\u1ea1i r\u1eb1ng n\u00f3 s\u1ebd [\u2026] l\u00e0m m\u1ea5t t\u00ednh trung gian c\u1ee7a h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng ng\u00e2n h\u00e0ng v\u00e0 \u0111e d\u1ecda s\u1ef1 \u1ed5n \u0111\u1ecbnh t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh, \u0111\u1ed3ng th\u1eddi, lo ng\u1ea1i r\u1eb1ng s\u1ebd kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng n\u00f3 v\u00e0 n\u00f3 s\u1ebd l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t 'gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p t\u00ecm ki\u1ebfm m\u1ed9t v\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1.\n For content creators, entrepreneurs, and anyone seeking to secure their financial future, understanding passive income is crucial. This article explores the meaning, importance, and the journey towards generating passive income.\n\n### What is Passive Income?\n\nPassive income is the revenue earned with minimal effort and ongoing involvement. Unlike active income, which is generated through your labor, time, or expertise, passive income streams allow you to make money while you sleep. These streams of income essentially work for you, freeing up your time and providing financial security.\n\nPassive income can come from various sources, including investments, businesses, and intellectual property. Here are some common examples:\n\n1. **Dividend Income:** Investing in dividend-paying stocks or mutual funds can generate regular dividends, providing a consistent passive income stream.\n\n2. **Rental Income:** Owning and renting out real estate properties, such as apartments, houses, or commercial spaces, can generate monthly rental income.\n\n3. **Royalties:** Authors, musicians, and inventors can earn royalties from their work, such as book sales, music downloads, or patent licensing.\n\n4. **Online Businesses:** Running an online business, dropshipping, or affiliate marketing can bring in passive income through automated sales and marketing processes.\n\n5. **Real Estate Investment Trusts (REITs):** REITs allow investors to pool their money and invest in a diversified portfolio of real estate properties, generating passive income from rental income and capital gains.\n\n### The Importance of Passive Income\n\nThe importance of passive income goes beyond financial stability; it represents a pathway to financial freedom and flexibility. Here are some key reasons why passive income is highly valued:\n\n1. **Financial Security:** Passive income can act as a safety net, helping you weather unexpected financial storms, such as medical emergencies or job loss.\n\n2. **Freedom of Time:** With passive income streams in place, you're not tied to a 9-to-5 job, giving you the freedom to allocate your time as you see fit.\n\n3. **Early Retirement:** Many individuals aim to retire early, and passive income can make this dream a reality by covering living expenses.\n\n4. **Wealth Accumulation:** Over time, passive income streams can grow, helping you accumulate wealth and potentially pass it on to future generations.\n\n5. **Diversification:** Relying solely on one source of income can be risky. Passive income diversifies your income streams, reducing dependence on a single source.\n\n6. **Work-Life Balance:** Passive income can help you achieve a healthier work-life balance by reducing the need for excessive hours of work.\n\n### The Journey Towards Passive Income\n\nAchieving passive income is a journey that requires dedication, knowledge, and effort. Here's a step-by-step guide to get you started:\n\n**1. Set Clear Goals:**\n   Define your financial goals and the level of passive income you want to achieve. Your goals will serve as motivation throughout your journey.\n\n**2. Assess Your Current Financial Situation:**\n   Take a close look at your existing income, expenses, and savings. Understanding your financial health is the first step in planning for passive income.\n\n**3. Create a Budget:**\n   Develop a budget that allows you to save and invest a portion of your active income. The money you save will be the capital you need to generate passive income.\n\n**4. Publish a book, create music, or invent something valuable and license it.\n\n**8. Automate Your Income Streams:**\n   Use automation tools and systems to manage your passive income streams efficiently. This can save you time and effort.\n\n**9. Monitor and Adjust:**\n   Regularly review your investments and income sources. Adjust your strategies as needed to optimize your passive income generation.\n\n**10. Be Patient:**\n   Building substantial passive income takes time and consistent effort. It's a long-term commitment that requires perseverance.\n\n### In Conclusion\n\nPassive income is not a get-rich-quick scheme, but rather a well-planned journey towards financial independence. It offers a path to financial security, freedom of time, and the opportunity to live life on your terms. Whether you're investing in stocks, running an online business, or creating intellectual property, understanding passive income is a critical step in securing your financial future. The results demonstrated that both Niacinamide and Clindamycin were effective in reducing acne.
